\doxysubsection{Constructor \& Destructor Documentation}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classokapi_1_1_chassis_controller_a8a4a431cb9da03a1c84e600dc0e31333}\label{classokapi_1_1_chassis_controller_a8a4a431cb9da03a1c84e600dc0e31333}} 
\index{okapi::ChassisController@{okapi::ChassisController}!ChassisController@{ChassisController}}
\index{ChassisController@{ChassisController}!okapi::ChassisController@{okapi::ChassisController}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ChassisController()}{ChassisController()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/6]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily okapi\+::\+Chassis\+Controller\+::\+Chassis\+Controller (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [explicit]}, {\ttfamily [default]}}

A \mbox{\hyperlink{classokapi_1_1_chassis_controller}{Chassis\+Controller}} adds a closed-\/loop layer on top of a \mbox{\hyperlink{classokapi_1_1_chassis_model}{Chassis\+Model}}. move\+Distance and turn\+Angle both use closed-\/loop control to move the robot. There are passthrough functions for everything defined in \mbox{\hyperlink{classokapi_1_1_chassis_model}{Chassis\+Model}}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em imodel} & underlying \mbox{\hyperlink{classokapi_1_1_chassis_model}{Chassis\+Model}} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classokapi_1_1_chassis_controller_a8a4a431cb9da03a1c84e600dc0e31333}\label{classokapi_1_1_chassis_controller_a8a4a431cb9da03a1c84e600dc0e31333}} 
\index{okapi::ChassisController@{okapi::ChassisController}!ChassisController@{ChassisController}}
\index{ChassisController@{ChassisController}!okapi::ChassisController@{okapi::ChassisController}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ChassisController()}{ChassisController()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/6]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily okapi\+::\+Chassis\+Controller\+::\+Chassis\+Controller (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [explicit]}, {\ttfamily [default]}}

A \mbox{\hyperlink{classokapi_1_1_chassis_controller}{Chassis\+Controller}} adds a closed-\/loop layer on top of a \mbox{\hyperlink{classokapi_1_1_chassis_model}{Chassis\+Model}}. move\+Distance and turn\+Angle both use closed-\/loop control to move the robot. There are passthrough functions for everything defined in \mbox{\hyperlink{classokapi_1_1_chassis_model}{Chassis\+Model}}.

{\em imodel} & underlying \mbox{\hyperlink{classokapi_1_1_chassis_model}{Chassis\+Model}} \\

\end{DoxyParams}
